package grhyph

import (
“fmt”
“regexp”
“strings”
)

// For a less error prone result, ‘h’ was removed from the vowels group, so that greeklish equivalents of
// words like “-” [khri’a] (where ‘h’ acts as a consonant) are hyphenated as hroi-a instead of
// h-roi-a [iria].
const SpeechSoundRe = “(?i)(?P[\s\.,\-\/’":!?;&@])|(?P[]|[a][uy]|[e][uy]|[i][uy]|[a][i]|[e][i]|[o][uy]|[o][i]|[a]|[e]|[i]|[i]|[o]|[yu]|[wo])|(?P(?:[m][p]|b)|(?:[g][k]|[g])|[n][tj]|[n]|(?:[8])|(?:[d])|(?:[tj][z]|j)|[z]|[tj][s]|[s][tj]|[v]|[l]|[m]|(?:ks|s|k|[x3])|[r]|[t]|[f]|[x]|ch|(?:[p][s]|[4])|[p]|[sc]|[k])|(?P[ns][tj]h+||.?)”

// Valid Greek word starting consonants.
// Important: Verify the getWSCRe()’s conditions when altering.
const WordStartConsonantsRe = “(?i)^(vb|g|(?:[t]h|[d])[n]|(?:[t]h|[d])[r]|(?:[t]h|[8])[lnr]|[k][vb]|[k][lnrtj]|[m][np]|[n][tj][^h]|[p][lnrtj]|[p][f]|s|[t][zmrs]|f|[f][k]|(?:[xh]|ch)(?:[8lnr]|[t]h?))”

type WSCReMapKey struct {
CombineConsonantsDn bool
CombineConsonantsKv bool
CombineConsonantsPf bool
CombineConsonantsFk bool
}

var WSCReMap = map[WSCReMapKey]regexp.Regexp{}

// Get a WordStartConsonantsRe based on the combination options.
func GetWSCRe(combDn, combKv, combPf, combFk bool) *regexp.Regexp {
mapKey := &WSCReMapKey{combDn, combKv, combPf, combFk}

if _, ok := WSCReMap[mapKey]; ok {
    return WSCReMap[mapKey]
} else {
    wSCRe := WordStartConsonantsRe

    if !combDn {
        wSCRe = strings.Replace(wSCRe, "|(?:[t]h|[d])[n]", "", 1)
    }
    if !combKv {
        wSCRe = strings.Replace(wSCRe, "|[k][vb]", "", 1)
    }
    if !combPf {
        wSCRe = strings.Replace(wSCRe, "|[p][f]", "", 1)
    }
    if !combFk {
        wSCRe = strings.Replace(wSCRe, "|[f][k]", "", 1)
    }

    WSCReMap[mapKey] = regexp.MustCompile(wSCRe)
    return WSCReMap[mapKey]
}

}

// Vowel combinations prone to synizesis.
const SynizesisVowelsRe = “(?i)^([a][hi]|[e][]|[e]i|i|o|[o]i|[uy][aiow])$”

type GrhyphRule struct {
CompiledCustomRe *regexp.Regexp
Replacement string
}

// Transforms the custom regexps into the canonical format, and compiles the result.
func customRegexpCompile(grhyphRegexps []string) *regexp.Regexp {
var canonRegexp []byte
canonRegexp = append(canonRegexp, “(?i)”…)

for _, grhyphRegexp := range grhyphRegexps {
    if mappedRe, ok := customRegexpsMap[grhyphRegexp]; ok {
        canonRegexp = append(canonRegexp, mappedRe...)
    } else {
        canonRegexp = append(canonRegexp, grhyphRegexp...)
        // debug
        fmt.Println("warning: custom regexp not found in map", grhyphRegexp) // todo: Error.
    }
}

return regexp.MustCompile(string(canonRegexp[:])) // todo: Error instead of panic.

}
